<p>The <b>2005 <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/FIFA_U-17_World_Championship" title="FIFA U-17 World Championship">FIFA U-17 World Championship</a></b>, the eleventh edition of the tournament, was held in the cities of <a href="/wiki/Lima" title="Lima">Lima</a>, <a href="/wiki/Trujillo,_Peru" title="Trujillo, Peru">Trujillo</a>, <a href="/wiki/Chiclayo" title="Chiclayo">Chiclayo</a>, <a href="/wiki/Piura" title="Piura">Piura</a> and <a href="/wiki/Iquitos" title="Iquitos">Iquitos</a> in <a href="/wiki/Peru" title="Peru">Peru</a> between 16 September and 2 October 2005. Players born after 1 January 1988 could participate in this tournament. Mexico beat favorite Brazil by 3–0 in the final, making it the first U-17 Championship for Mexico.</p>
<p></p>

<ul>
<li>USA is the only team to have qualified for all 11 tournaments so far, followed by Brazil and Australia who have each qualified 10 times. While Netherlands, Turkey, Peru, Gambia and Korea DPR are new to the competition.</li>
</ul>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Goalscorers">Goalscorers</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2005_FIFA_U-17_World_Championship&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Goalscorers">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-scorers_1-0"><a href="#cite_note-scorers-1">[1]</a></sup></p>
<p>Carlos Vela of Mexico won the <a href="/wiki/FIFA_U-17_World_Cup#Awards" title="FIFA U-17 World Cup">Golden Shoe</a> award for scoring five goals. In total, 111 goals were scored by 67 different players, with four of them credited as own goals.</p>
<dl>
<dt>5 goals</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/Mexico" title="Mexico"><img alt="Mexico" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="480" data-file-width="840" height="13" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fc/Flag_of_Mexico.svg/23px-Flag_of_Mexico.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fc/Flag_of_Mexico.svg/35px-Flag_of_Mexico.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fc/Flag_of_Mexico.svg/46px-Flag_of_Mexico.svg.png 2x" width="23"/></a></span> <a href="/wiki/Carlos_Vela" title="Carlos Vela">Carlos Vela</a></li>
</ul>
<dl>
<dt>4 goals</dt>
</dl>
<ul>
<li><span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/Brazil" title="Brazil"><img alt="Brazil" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="504" data-file-width="720" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/0/05/Flag_of_Brazil.svg/22px-Flag_of_Brazil.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/0/05/Flag_of_Brazil.svg/33px-Flag_of_Brazil.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/0/05/Flag_of_Brazil.svg/43px-Flag_of_Brazil.svg.png 2x" width="22"/></a></span> <a href="/wiki/Igor_Siqueira_Pessanha" title="Igor Siqueira Pessanha">Igor</a></li>
